Categories

    Console Commands

    CommandDescriptionExample
    advlevelInstant level up
    coc <Location>Teleport to Location. You can find a list of all the Locations in the game lower in the guidecoc WeynonPrioryHouse
    GhostFly through walls and become invicible (like a ghost)
    KillWhile the console is open, press on a character and use this cheat to kill them
    KillAllKill everyone around
    movetoqtMove to the current selected quest’s objective
    ObvGodModeActivates Overpowered God Mode (invincibility, money, max skills and stats)
    player.additem 0000000B 1Get Skeleton Key which unlocks any door
    player.additem f 1000000Add money. In this case 1 million
    player.AddItem <ItemID Amount>Add a new item to your inventory. Change <ItemID>with an actual ID and the Amount with a number to get that item in your inventoryplayer.AddItem 00014D66 1
    player.addspell <SpellID>Learn a new spell. Change <SpellID>with the spell’s ID you want to learnplayer.addspell 000A97F9
    player.advskill <Skill Amount>Set the skill to the desired amount. Write the skill names exactly the same as they appear in the menus, two word skills are written in one wordplayer.advskill heavyarmor 100
    player.modav encumbrance –<Amount>Increase carry weightplayer.modav encumbrance -9999
    player.setav <Attribute Amount>Set the attribute (strength, intelligence, willpower, agility, speed, endurance, personality, or luck) to the desired amountplayer.setav strength 250
    psbUnlock all spells
    ShowBirthsignMenuChange Birthsign
    ShowClassMenuChange class (resets skills)
    ShowEnchantmentEnchant equipment
    ShowRaceMenuChange appearance
    ShowSpellMakingCreate Spells
    SkipTutorialQuestImmediately end the Tutorial Quest. You’ll still have to teleport out of the prison
    taiActivates (or deactivates) the AI
    tcaiActivates (or deactivates) the AI’s ability to fight
    tdetectActivates (or deactivates) the AI’s ability to detect you
    tgmActivates God Mode (invincibility)
    tmm 1Unlock all Map Markers (tmm 0 hides all markers)
    ToggleDebugCameraToggle debug photo mode
    UnlockWhile the console is open, press on a door and use this cheat to unlock it
    WalkReverse the Ghost cheat
    ShowentriesPage 1

    All Toggle Commands

    CommandDescription
    Altar.GraphicsOptions.HDR 1Enable HDR support
    ghostToggle collision (clipping, noclip). “walk” will disable this one
    pcbPurge cell buffer
    showsubtitleToggles NPC conversation subtitles
    taiToggle AI
    tcaiToggle combat AI
    tdetectToggle AI detection
    tdtToggle debug text
    tfcFreeflying camera
    tfhToggle full help
    tfowToggle fog of war
    tgToggle grass
    tgmToggle god mode
    tllToggle land LOD (level of detail)
    tlvToggle leaves
    tmToggles menus (HUD)
    tmgToggle material geometry
    tmm <Amount>Show(1)/hide(0) all map markers
    tsToggle sky
    ttToggle trees
    twfToggle wireframe mode
    twrToggle water radius
    twsToggle water rendering
    ShowentriesPage 1

    Target Commands

    CommandDescription
    additem <ItemID Amount>Add item to inventory. There’s a long list of IDs lower in the guide
    addspell <SpellID>Add spell. There’s a long list of IDs lower in the guide
    createfullactorcopyClones target actor
    deletefullactorcopyDeletes a clone of the target actor
    dispel <SpellID>Dispel a specific magic effect from target
    dispelallspellsDispel all spell-based magic effects from target
    equipitem <ItemID>Equip an Item
    getav <attribute>Get value of attribute
    getBarterGoldGets the target’s shop gold
    getcrimegoldGets the target’s current bounty.
    kill <NPCID>Kill NPC. You can also just write “kill” and press the target with your mouse
    lock <Amount>Lock doors or chests. The amount is the difficutly from 1 to 99
    moddisposition <NPCID Amount>Change NPC disposition
    moveto <ID>Teleports you to destination. The ID can be either an object or an NPC
    payfinePay criminal fines
    payfinethiefPay criminal fines without removing stolen items
    placeatme <ID>Spawns a copy of ID in front of you
    removeitem <ItemID Amount>Remove item from inventory
    removespell <SpellID>Remove spell
    resurrect 1Resurrects target. NPCs might still refer to the target as dead if you didn’t do it immediately after death
    SetActorFullName <Name>Change your name. Use quotation marks if you want to have spaces in your name
    setav <attribute Amount>Sets value of attribute
    setBarterGold <Amount>Sets the target’s shop gold.
    setcrimegold <Amount>Sets bounty on target
    setessential <ID Amount>Sets the target’s essential flag. 1 is essential, 0 is non-essential
    setlevel <Amount>Changes target’s level
    SetOwnership [<ID>/<FactionID>]Changes ownership of targeted item to you (if no ID is specified), or to the specified NPC/Faction
    setscale <Amount>Change target height (1 is human)
    startcombat <NPCID>Start target combat
    stopcombatStop target combat
    unlockUnlock doors or chests
    ShowentriesPage 1

    Quest Commands

    CommandDescription
    caqsCompletes all quest stages (will likely crash your game)
    completequest <QuestID>Completes quest
    GetStage <QuestID>Shows quest stage for <QuestID>
    movetoqtTeleport to quest target
    player.completequest <QuestID>Removes quest from list. (Does not complete it)
    SetStage <QuestID> <StageID>Advances <QuestID> to <StageID>. Useful for bugged quests. Only works if you use “Altar.Cheat.AllowSetStage true” command beforehand
    showfullquestlog <QuestID>Shows all log entries for <QuestID>
    showquestlogShow quest log
    showquestlog 0Show current quest log
    showquestlog 1Show completed quest log
    ShowQuestTargetsShows active quests ID and stage
    sqShow all quests and stage
    sqtShow current quest
    ShowentriesPage 1
